[MBO-07-1]
<H>{@sāraḷā mahābhārata@}
<H>{@bhīṣmapac bonṅa@}
<H>{@gaṇeśaṅka bandanā@}
<P>jaẏatu dadhimaṅgaḷa jaẏa bighnarāja
<P>draśane mukati ye prasanne karu siddha sac bonṅakāryya | 1 |
<P>saṃsiddha puruṣa tu sac bonṅadā rase bhoḷa
<P>muhiṃ tote bheṭili śwetagaṅgara kūḷa | 2 |
<P>ādi abatāre śūdrika nāme brahmā
<P>aneka kāḷa bañthāilī yebaṇa mahātamā | 3 |
<P>bharaharaṣa nāyaka nṛtyarase bheḷā
<P>mahārase rasika nātha tāṇḍaba nṛtyakaḷā | 4 |
<P>sita pīta kuṃkuma yāra śirare sitāṃśu
<P>dinakara teja harai yāhāra śrībhuje tīkhaparaśu | 5 |
<P>yogānanda puruṣa tu bale mahāmeru
<P>tu yāku prasanna gata āgata tāku ṣphuru | 6 |
<P>swāmī kārttaka prahāra ye kale bāma pādaghāte
<P>daṣi ṇa danta bhagnagalī anujara kopa catte | 7 |
<P>se bhagnadanta paḍḍalī upare pṛthī se bhagnadantabhare | 8 |
[MBO-07-2]
<H1>{@mahābharata@}
<P>yahuṃ se baḍa ārata hoilī dharaṇī
<P>basudhā rāsāiṅgate tusti kale śūḷapāṇi | 9 |
<P>sacarācara pṛthrabīki ḍaddhara parśupāṇi
<P>bāma bhmaje saṃharaṇa nātha kalu tāhā āṇi | 10 |
<P>kope śāpya tāku dilu ye turite
<P>galūta kuṣṭhabyādhna hoilā kārttikara | 11 |
<P>drodakarma kalī na galī tāku pāra
<P>rakta māṃse pūtta gaddha bahai rudhira | 12 |
<P>hara pābonṅatī boile doṣa kalu ẏamā
<P>tā kaṣga dekhi daẏākala ye mahātmā | 13 |
<P>kopa śānti yeṇu nuāriī tohora
<P>galūta kuṣṭhabyādhi hoilā kārtikara | 14 |
<P>taba kara līgante hoilīka rakṣā
<P>āpāda śānti kari ruhāilu kaya | 15 |
<P>amr̥ta bhejane to śarīra traputi
<P>abhaẏe puruṣa tu gajānana mūrtta | 16 |
<P>raṇa jhaṇa śabada to caraṇe nūpura
<P>calilīka medinī tohora pādabhīra | 17 |
<P>aṅga rakta barṇṇa sahiṣṇu ye meru
<P>brahmāṇḍa mampai bājante yāhāra ḍamwaru | 18 |
<P>bijighoṣa śai tāḷa ye kaṃsāḷi
<P>jhaṭake mohilu tuhi deba ye kāpālī | 19 |
<P>meru tulya maḍali ārakta varṇṇa ākhi
<P>apachhag br̥nda bhajile tohora tāṇḍaba nr̥tya dekhi | 20 |
[MBO-07-3]
<P>śrībhmae saraguṇā tāḷa ye adhāṭi
<P>susware gītarase ārambha nr̥tya heṭi | 21 |
<P>rāra rājā māḷaba lalita basanta bhirobī
<P>mālaśrī nārāẏaṇī gaurī maṅkaḷabarāḍi mālaba gauḍi raṅke bhībi
<P>nāgaballī karṇṇāṭī gujjarī bhūpāḷa
<P>mahlāra amara raṅkeṇa handoḷa | 23 |
<P>yāmaḷā toḍi bibhāsa bicitra deṣī baṅgaḷāśrī
<P>rāga rājā dhanāśrī deṣī deśāṣa cintā miśi | 24 |
<P>gujjigī mahlāra kalyīṇī paṭahamañjarī
<P>kāśī kanaḍā kauśika ābhirī guṇḍakerī | 25 |
<P>kedāra basantabagḍi madhukegī toḍi
<P>baṅgāḷa chekhi ābara pañchambarāḍi | 26 |
<P>biṣhnura gāẏeṇī śate kanyāṃkara mūḷe
<P>khaṭanti bilāsuṇī nr̥tya raṅgarasa bheḷe | 27 |
<P>guṇasāgara nātha bheleṇa mahāprahu
<P>asaṃkhya mahimā sañṣepi heba kāhuṃ | 28 |
<P>yāhāra nṛtyaku abadhārī br̥ndāarke
<P>mohilu sadānanda swāmī bhajile nāgaloke | 29 |
<P>ananta nāga indranātha mekhaḷā śobhi kaṭi
<P>nāśilu sabon pāpa hṛdagate ghoṣiṇa taba nāma goṭi | 30 |
<P>śrī bighnagjaṃka caraṇa sebā mohora hṛde
<P>bañchali kr̥tāntaka bhaẏaru nātha tohora parasāde | 31 |
<P>manmatha sundara nīḷendī yāra barṇṇa
<P>draśane harai sakaḷa bighnamāna | 32 |

[MBO-07-4]
<H>{@śiba o biṣṇuṅkara staba@}
<P>jaẏa jayḷa nātha kāmenī mohana manasija
<P>bighaṃsita kamala birājai yāhāra pāda paṃkaja | 1 |
<P>yoge yogeśwara tu prasanne parama rūpa
<P>hele nibārilu kr̥tāntaka darpa | 2 |
<P>paṇṭita janaṃkara hr̥de tu kamala puṣwamāli
<P>surasiddha muni meḷe śobhita kapālī | 3 |
<P>tu deba saẏaḷa jībara cintāmaṇi
<P>to pāda paṃkaje bhajanti parśupāṇi | 4 |
<P>birañchi ballabha parama yogeśwara
<P>mama mana raha to caraṇa kamaḷa | 5 |
<P>akāma akāḷa amoha jaḷa phāśī
<P>ẏethuṃ uddhari mote mukti patha desi | 6 |
<P>apaṇḍita mūrkha muṃ ntahai baḍa gyāṃtā
<P>śrī puruṣottama nāma muṃ ddhāneṇa bhagatā | 7 |
<P>kālindī kamaḷa prāẏe bikaca mukha goṭi
<P>ihajanna bhabe muṃ pāibiji bheṭi | 8 |
<P>bhārathīra ballabha kamaḷāra prāṇabaddhu
<P>sañsāra andhakāre tumbhe aṭa indu | 9 |
<P>daibakī nandana yaśodā pratipāḷi
<P>aṣṭamalla niśodhana nāma to banamāḷī | 10 |
<P>bāma kare kamwu daṣiṇe sundra śena
<P>narktuṃ tāraṇa nātha nāma to janārddana | 11 |

[MBO-07-5]
<P>yamanika tīrthe bheṭili muṃ tote

<H>{@bhīṣmaṅka nikaṭare purehitaṅkara annadāna kathā barṇṇana@}
<P>baibasuta manu āge badaẏanti agasti
<P>arjunaku samārjanā kari āsanti śrīpati | 1 |
<P>bijaẏe dharma nandana indrapraśastare
<P>birase paśile yāiṃ ye yāhā mandire | 2 |
<P>srāhāna nityakarma sāriṇa deba pukā
<P>pitr̥ āhānika sāri muṇohire bije debarājā | 3 |
<P>śuṇa ho baibasuta manu kaureba saini
<P>sādhu sādhu bhīṣme coli śubhilā mukha dhuni | 4 |
<P>aneka arghya bandābanti bhīṣmaṃkara māthe
<P>laṣe ratna gheni srāhāna karāile kurunāthe | 5 |
<P>ẏemante samara karante daśadina niti

<P1>203 {labha tu aneka śirī mama kailāṇa tote bāñchā
<>ẏekamane pañchusthaḷī bhegyakara tu kaicthā?? | (jha,ṅa)}
<P1>203|2 kaṣā--pratiñṅka,kīrtti |
[MBO-07-329]
<H>{@bhīṣmaparbara adhikā pāṭha@}
<H1>320 pr̥ṣṭhā 1072 pāṭha pare "dha" pothire:-
<P>śrīkhaṇḍī dhr̥ṣṭaketu ye hoilā sāṃgrāma
<P>bhīṣme sāṃgrāma kale hoiṇa abiśrāma | 1 |
<P>sañjaẏa bolanti ho dhr̥tirāṣṭa rāṇa
<P>daśa dina yudda karile gaṅgāṅka nandana | 2 |
<P>droṇa arjunara sāṃgrāma heuacchi
<P>abhimanyu aśastamā paḍilā pañchā pañchi |  3 |
<P>caitana rājā tule śakunira yuda
<P>citrasena bikarṇṇara lāgilā bibāda | 4|
<P>bhīmasena karṇṇa beni karucchanti raṇa
<P>dhuśāsana durddaṣa samara anyeanya | 5 |
<P>driyodhana tule yudda karanti yujheṣṭhi
<P>śagka ulukara hoilāka ariṣṭi | 6 |
<P>śrīkhaṇḍī bhāṣma āge hoilaka ubha
<P>ṣudhārtti yesaneke miṣṭānne kare lobha | 7 |
<P>rāhura teja jāṇi bhīṣmanta ākarṣi
<P>nārabaḷa dekhi yehne binatā putra grāsi | 8 |
<P>ḍākai pacharu pārtha śara bidha re śrīkhaṇḍī
<P>tora pacche muhiṃ acchi nandighoṣa maṇḍi | 9 |
<P>sāhā pāi mārai se dr̥pada tanaẏe
<P>bhīṣaṇa śara paḍe megha br̥ṣṭi prāẏe | 10 |
<P>ẏemanta dekhi bhīṣme śrīkhaṇḍī praśaṃsanti
<P>stirīḷiṅga hoi tora ẏeḍeka śakati | 11 |
[MBO-07-330]
<P>ẏeḍe baḍa aṭu tuhi cchatriẏa mahābaḷā
<P>mohora hetu tote daiba nirmāṇilā | 12 |
<P>bhīṣmaṃku bolai yahuṃ pāṇḍaba dhanurjaẏe
<P>dekhi niṣata hoile bhīṣma mahārāẏe | 13 |
<P>muṃ tote sañpaṣa tu na karasi bhaẏe
<P>bhīṣma nāśile āmbhara heba raṇa jaẏe | 14 |
<P>bhīṣma aśastamā ẏe dui mahārathā
<P>harihara brahmāra ẏe chedi pāranti mathā | 15 |
<P>droṇa kr̥pāchāryye nr̥pati kurunātha
<P>chatrībara sāmaratha khaṭanti jagata | 16 |
<P>driyodhana boilā ye bhīṣma mukha chāhiṃ
<P>uprodha yudda swāmī karuccha kisa pāiṃ | 17 |
<P>daẏāpaṇa chaḍi ẏebe pāṇḍabanta māra
<P>tumbhe parā kurubaḷe aṭa dhanurddara| 18 |
<P>bhīṣme boile rājā he sarūpa kahuṃ tote
<P>yudde baḷīyāra kehu kaha mo agrate | 19 |
<P>laṣeka yoddā āmbhe māilu daśadine
<P>aśwa gaja jete male ke karu kaḷane | 20 |
<P>arjuna jiṇi tote rājya debāpāiṃ
<P>ẏe kathā bolucchu ki kaha re kurusāiṃ | 21 |
<P>āja ẏadde āmbhe māribu pāṇḍacanta
<P>daiba keuṃ kathā karicchi tā na jāṇi tadanta | 22 |
<P>ẏeteka boliṇa se dhanure khūrpa daśabāṇa sadha
<P>dr̥ṣṭigocara acchi śrīkhaṇḍī mahāyodhī | 23 |
<P>śuṇa ho aśastamā boile gaṅgāsuta
<P>āja mora na caḷai kimpāiṃ karapatra | 24 |
<P>ratha dhwaje basilāṇi mora gr̥dhra pacchī
<P>dekha mora naẏanaru lotaka bahr̥acchi | 25 |
[MBO-07-331]
<P>dekha ho troṇe mora nārāja nāhiṃ kicchi
<P>bajra guṇa mora dhanuru cchiṇḍicchi | 26 |
<P>tuhāi bidhai śrīkhaṇḍī bhīṣmaṃka uparaku
<P>goṭi goṭi bidhai se marma sthānaṭhāku | 27 |
<P>śrikhaṇḍīki paccha kari dhāmaiṃ kirīṭī
<P>pāṇḍaba yoddāmāne aile sabonṅa ghoṭi | 28 |
<P>śrīkhaṇḍīki āga kari arjuna thāi pacche
<P>nirghāta bāṇa bidhe bajrara sāriṣe | 29 |
<P>br̥ṣṭi parāẏe śara se paḍe bhīṣmaṃkara aṅge
<P>bikarāḷa hoiṇa uṭhileka gāṅgabe | 30 |
<P>pāśare thilā tāṃkara rājā driyodhana
<P>bege āgyāṃ dilā chāre gādhārī nandana | 31 |
<P>samare arjuna ye ātroṣe bhīṣmaṃku
<P>hakāri āṇa mora bhāi ye mānaṃku | 32 |
<P>āgyāṃ pāiṇa ḍagara bega hoi galā
<P>śatebhāi karṇṇa ādi rāiṇa āṇilā | 33 |
<P>droṇa kr̥pa sahitare rājā bhagadatta
<P>arjune beḍhile se gheniṇa śahasranta | 34 |
<P>beni baḷa bheṭante se bājilā raṇagoḷa
<P>māra māra ḍākare ye ārai dhandoḷa | 35 |
<P>praḷaẏa kāḷe yehne sāhera laharā
<P>benibaḷa thāṭha ye temanta diśilā | 36 |
<P>śara ātayāteṇa ye hoilā adhāra
<P>bhīṣmaṃkara teja tahiṃ yesane dinakara | 37 |
<P>anibonṅāraṇa yoddā se gaṅgāra kumara
<P>nimiśeke kāṭile śate rājāṃkara śira | 38 |
<P>puṇa sātabāṇa bidhale se tuhāi
<P>hāthara byagra tāṃkara bacane nohe kahi | 39 |
<P1>352 āraṇi--yudda |
[MBO-07-332]
<P>sātalaṣa yoddā se kāṭile tataṣaṇa
<P>bhārathe sama nāhiṃ ẏe bhīṣmaṃka samāna | 40 |
<P>dekhiṇa ajuna ye hoilāka rāga
<P>bāhile turaṅgame deba ye śrīraṅga | 41 |

<P>marmasthānamānanta bidhai manabhedī | 44 |
<P>puṇa bidhai se śara jāḷābaḷī
<P>bhīṣmara de?? ye se kāṭilā nireḷi | 45 |
<P>kehi na dekhanti pārtha bidhuacchi śara
<P>bhīṣmaṃkara deha goṭi rudhire jarajara | 46 |
<P>yuṇihiṃ chaḍabāṇa arjuna bidhalā

<P>ẏeṇe bāṇamāna bahuta paḍe dehe
<P>tāhā na māniṇa śara bidhacchanti kohe | 51 |
<P>aneka beḷa arjuna cchedalāka tanu
<P>rāgeṇa khaṇḍā dhaile gaṅgādebī tanu | 52 |
<P>agniśikhā jāṇi tāṃka kare karabāḷa
<P>hārtharu cchedilā tā bāsaba dulāḷa | 53 |
[MBO-07-333]
<P>puṇa dhanu dharante tā cchedilā arjuna
<P>bhīṣmaṃku ābori ye acchanti kuru saina | 54 |
<P>ẏemanta samaẏare arjuna śara māri
<P>marmathaḷe paḍilā se nohilā nibāri | 55 |

<P>prasanne bara yāku deicchi sadāśiba
